    <div onclick="" class="rebirth-card r-card301"></div>
    <span>
      <p class="item-title">Rebirth Pills P - Z (Page 2 of 2)</p>
      <p>&#8226; Paralysis - Prevents you from moving for a short while</p>
      <p>&#8226; Pheromones - Applies the charm effect to all enemies in the room for a short while</p>
      <p>&#8226; Puberty - Causes Isaac to grow hair for the rest of the run. Cosmetic change only. In Afterbirth+, taking 3 of this pill gives the Adult transformation</p>
      <p>&#8226; Pretty Fly - Gives Isaac +1 fly orbital, which blocks enemy projectiles and damages fly-type enemies on touch</p>
      <p>&#8226; Range Down - Reduces your range stat by -2</p>
      <p>&#8226; Range Up - Increases your range stat by +2.5</p>
      <p>&#8226; R U a wizard? - Tears will shoot diagonally for about 60 seconds. Effect persists between rooms while the time period is active</p>
      <p>&#8226; Speed Down - Reduces your speed stat by -0.12</p>
      <p>&#8226; Speed Up - Increases your speed stat by +0.15</p>
      <p>&#8226; Tears Down - Reduces your tears stat by -0.28</p>
      <p>&#8226; Tears Up - Increases your tears stat by 0.35</p>
      <p>&#8226; Telepills - Teleports you to a random room when used. Has a small chance to take you to the I AM ERROR room, and a smaller chance to teleport to a Black Market</p>
      <p class="tags">* </p>
    </span>
  </a>
</li>
<li class="textbox dlccontent condensed" data-tid="1002" data-sid="1002">
  <a>
    <div onclick="" class="rebirth-card r-card302"></div>
    <span>
      <p class="item-title">Afterbirth Pills</p>
      <p>&#8226; Addicted - Causes you to take a full heart of damage for all sources for the current room. Unlocked from Challenge #24 - PAY TO PLAY</p>
      <p>&#8226; Friends till the end - Spawns three friendly blue attack flies</p>
      <p>&#8226; Infested! - Destroys all poops in the room and spawns a blue attack spider on every destroyed poop</p>
      <p>&#8226; Infested? - Spawns one blue attack spider for every enemy in the room. If there are no enemies this pill spawns 1-3 blue spiders instead</p>
      <p>&#8226; One makes you smaller - Reduces Isaac's size and hitbox size</p>
      <p>&#8226; One makes you larger - Increases Isaac's size, but does not affect the size of his hitbox</p>
      <p>&#8226; Percs - Causes Isaac to only take half a heart of damage from all sources for the current room (The Wafer effect). Unlocked from Challenge #24 - PAY TO PLAY</p>
      <p>&#8226; Power Pill - Gives you invulnerability and the ability to damage enemies for a short while (similar to The Gamekid effect)</p>
      <p>&#8226; Re-Lax - Causes Isaac to spawn poops behind him while he walks for a few seconds. Similar to Explosive Diarrhea but with poop</p>
      <p>&#8226; Retro Vision - Pixelates the screen for a few seconds, obscuring your vision. Happens a total of 3 times over 30 seconds</p>
      <p>&#8226; ??? - Gives the curse of the maze effect for the current floor. Unlocked from Challenge #25 - Have a Heart</p>
      <p class="tags">* </p>
    </span>
  </a>
</li>
<li class="textbox dlccontentplus condensed" data-tid="1003" data-sid="1003">
  <a>
    <div onclick="" class="rebirth-card r-card303"></div>
    <span>
      <p class="item-title">Afterbirth+ Pills</p>
      <p>&#8226; Feels like I'm walking on sunshine! - Turns Isaac invincible for a few seconds (similar to Unicorn Stump). Unlocked from the 'Sin Collector' achievement (collect every Bestiary entry)</p>
      <p>&#8226; Gulp! - When used will consume your current trinket, destroying it and giving you its effect permanently. Unlocked from the 'Once more with the feeling!' achievement (complete a victory lap, defeating the lamb boss)</p>
      <p>&#8226; Horf! - When used, shoots an Ipecac explosive shot. Unlocked from the 'Dedication' achievement (participate in 31 dailies in a row)</p>
      <p>&#8226; I'm Drowsy... - Slows all enemies for the rest of the current room</p>
      <p>&#8226; I'm excited!!! - Speeds up all enemies for the rest of the room. The effect triggers again 30 seconds after use and again 60 seconds after use</p>
      <p>&#8226; Something's wrong... - Spawns a pool of black creep beneath Isaac</p>
      <p>&#8226; Vurp! - Spawns the last pill you used. Spawns another Vurp! pill if no other pills were used yet. Unlocked from the 'U broke it!' achievement (collect 50 items in a single run)</p>
      <p>&#8226; X-Lax - Spawns a pool of slippery brown creep beneath Isaac</p>
      <p class="tags">* </p>
    </span>
  </a>
</li>
